class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">It's been four years since Donald Trump made a string of promises during his long 2016 campaign to be the 45th president of the United States. Four years later, his supporters often cite "promises made, promises kept" as a reason why they're backing him again. </b></p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Many of them made headlines - from banning all Muslims entering the US, to building a border wall paid for by Mexico.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">But others went a little under the radar, like his pledge to eliminate the national debt.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">So how has he done in keeping his promises?</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before election: </b>Trump promised to lower the corporate tax rate and bring in huge tax cuts for working Americans.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>The Republican tax plan passed in December 2017, and it largely ticks the box for the president although its merits are hotly disputed. He has had to compromise on his pledge to bring corporation tax down from 35% to 15% (it will be 21% instead). </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">And the tax cuts for individuals will expire, although Republicans say future governments will simply renew them. But wealthy Americans are expected to benefit more than poorer ones. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Not everyone saw their taxes lowered. For some higher earners in urbanised, mostlyDemocraticstates, taxes went up due to a cap on state and local property and income tax deductions.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before: </b>One of Mr Trump's trademark rally pledges was to repeal and replace Obamacare - his predecessor's attempt to extend healthcare to the estimated 15% of the country who are not covered.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">It is widely hated by Republicans, who say the law imposes too many costs on business, with many describing it as a "job killer" and decrying the reforms - officially the Affordable Care Act - as an unwarranted intrusion into the affairs of private businesses and individuals.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>Republicans have been unable to pass a repeal or reform bill.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">That said, the Trump administration has managed to dismantle parts of the law - enrolment periods have been shortened, some subsidies have been axed, and the fine for people who did not purchase health insurance has been eliminated as part of the 2017 tax plan.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">And in December 2018, a federal judge in Texas ruled that repealing this penalty, an "essential" part of the law, meant the entirety of Obamacare is therefore unconstitutional.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The law, however, remains in place as an appeal heads to the US Supreme Court, with a ruling expected sometime in 2021. </p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="media-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before: </b>His vow to build a wall along the US-Mexican border was one of the most controversial of Mr Trump's campaign promises. Mr Trump also insisted that Mexico would pay for it.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>Mexico poured scorn on the claim that it would pay for such a barrier, and even Mr Trump appears to have dropped that idea.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Democrats are vociferously opposed to a wall, whereas some Republicans have baulked at a bill that could reach $21.5bn (17bn), according to a Department of Homeland Security internal report.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">In December 2018 the US government went into shutdown after Democrats resisted Mr Trump's demands for $5bn to fund the wall. He has since redirected defence and some other funds to build or replace sections of the wall, a decision that has faced legal challenges. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">As of late May, 194 miles of wall system had been built, mostly to shore up dilapidated or outdated designs of the barrier already in place - just three miles construction was part of an entirely new system. spending increased dramatically from 2002 as the US entered protracted wars in Iraq and Afghanistan. It peaked in 2010 as a percentage of GDP - the value of all goods and services - after which the US began stepping back from its engagement in the Middle East and Central Asia. </p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><div class="ssrcss-h5qd1q-ListContainer e5tfeyi0"><ul class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="Cutting-regulations" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">Cutting regulations</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-138qy0m-Placeholder etlorgc0"><picture><source class="ssrcss-11yxrdo-Image edrdn950" height="50" loading="lazy" src="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/640/cpsprodpb/165EA/production/_114162619_delivered_640x50-nc.png" https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/480/cpsprodpb/165EA/production/_114162619_delivered_640x50-nc.png 480w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/624/cpsprodpb/165EA/production/_114162619_delivered_640x50-nc.png 624w" width="640"/></picture></span></div></figure></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before:</b> Just a month before his election win in November 2016, Mr Trump said he could cut as many as 70% of US federal regulations if elected. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">"It's just stopping businesses from growing," <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/election-us-2016-37582318">he told an audience in New Hampshire</a>. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The promise drew him support from large and small businesses, who helped him to victory that year. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>The president has slashed through regulations on everything from labour to the environment.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Just days after taking office he signed the Presidential Executive Order on Reducing Regulation and Controlling Regulatory Costs, which mandated that when government departments asked for a federal regulation, they had to specify two others they would drop. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Throughout his term he has continued to slash back red tape. In January 2020 he scrapped protections for US wetlands and streams, and in July he announced changes to the National Environmental Protection Act in a bid to speed up infrastructure projects. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">"We are reclaiming America's proud heritage as a nation that gets things done," he said. </p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><div class="ssrcss-h5qd1q-ListContainer e5tfeyi0"><ul role="list"><li><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/business-54303682">'Trump's done what he said he would for business'</a></p></li><li><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/election-us-2020-54103861">Five things Trump has said about the environment</a></p></li></ul></div></div></div><div id="piano-inline3"></div><div class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="Bringing-troops-home" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">Bringing troops home</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-138qy0m-Placeholder 480w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/624/cpsprodpb/3152/production/_114162621_pd_640x50-nc.png 624w" width="640"/></picture></span></div></figure></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before:</b> Mr Trump has long called for the US to leave the Middle East. On the 2016 campaign trail, he said the region was a "total and complete mess" and wished the government had spent the trillions of dollars in the US instead.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">His talk of an end to US military deployments overseas predates his presidential run. In 2013, he tweeted: "Our troops are being killed by the Afghanis we train and we waste billions there. Nonsense! Rebuild the USA." That same year, he said the US should "stay the hell out" of the Syrian war. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>In September 2017, the Trump administration announced the deployment of 3,000 additional troops to Afghanistan. Mr Trump said his approach would be based on conditions on the ground. In Syria, the US had led a coalition against IS along with Syrian Kurdish and Arab fighters, with around 2,000 troops on the ground.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">By December 2018, Mr Trump ordered the withdrawal of all US troops from Syria, though about half the troops, approximately 500, still remain. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Mr Trump recently said he has plans to further cut troops in Afghanistan - after reducing them to 8,600 from 13,000 over the spring and summer  - before the 3 November election. In February, US and Nato allies agreed to withdraw all troops from the country within 14 months if Taliban militants uphold a new peace agreement.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The president's efforts to pull down troops has at times been met with criticism from his own officials. Following Mr Trump's announcement of a Syria withdrawal <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/world-us-canada-46644841">in part prompted the resignation of US Defence Secretary James Mattis</a>. </p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><div class="ssrcss-h5qd1q-ListContainer e5tfeyi0"><ul role="list"><li><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/world-middle-east-46626115">Trump rewrites US Syria policy</a></p></li><li><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/world-asia-51689443">US and Taliban sign deal to end 18-year Afghan war</a></p></li></ul></div></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-ciorxc-Placeholder class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="Trade-deals" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">Trade deals</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before: </b>Mr Trump called Nafta "a disaster" and warned that the TPP "is going to be worse, so we will stop it". He also pledged to correct the trade deficit with China.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>Mr Trump followed through in his first few days on his pledge to withdraw from the Trans Pacific Partnership (TPP). He later said he would consider re-joining the TPP if he got a better deal.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">On 30 November, after protracted negotiations, the US, Canada and Mexico signed the US-Mexico-Canada Agreement, which was designed to replace Nafta and recently came into force. However, the US has reimposed aluminium tariffs on Canada, and Ottawa reciprocated with retaliatory tariffs. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The US and South Korea also signed a revised trade pact in September 2018. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The US and China, meanwhile, became embroiled in an escalating trade battle - with both sides imposing tariffs on billions of dollars' worth of goods. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Despite ongoing tensions, in August the US and China held talks over their <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/business-51114425">so-called "phase-one" trade deal - signed early this year</a> - that is aimed at easing the trade war. </p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><div class="ssrcss-h5qd1q-ListContainer e5tfeyi0"><ul class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="/news/business-53900054">US and China hold 'constructive' trade talks</a></p></li></ul></div></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div src="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/464/cpsprodpb/0D91/production/_92437430_line976.jpg" srcset="https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/240/cpsprodpb/0D91/production/_92437430_line976.jpg 240w, https://ichef.bbci.co.uk/ace/standard/320/cpsprodpb/0D91/production/_92437430_line976.jpg 320w" width="464"/></picture></span><span class="ssrcss-2z7a81-StyledFigureCopyright e34k3c20" role="text"><span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">Image source, </span>AFP</span></div></figure></div><div class="ssrcss-1o1fzgd-ComponentWrapper-HeadlineComponentWrapper egtrm1f0" data-component="subheadline-block"><h2 class="ssrcss-pbttu9-Heading e10rt3ze0" id="Ban-on-Muslims" tabindex="-1"><span role="text">Ban on Muslims</span></h2></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure class="ssrcss-12gl1u2-StyledFigure e34k3c22"><div class="ssrcss-ab5fd8-StyledFigureContainer e34k3c21"><span class="ssrcss-138qy0m-Placeholder etlorgc0"><picture><source class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before: </b>Mr Trump initially promised to ban all Muslims entering the US - a "total and complete" shutdown should remain until the US authorities "can figure out what's going on".</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">But he switched to "extreme vetting" after he became the party's presidential candidate. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>As president, he introduced two travel bans which became ensnarled in the courts - but the third had more luck. The US Supreme Court ruled President Trump's ban on six mainly Muslim countries can go into full effect, pending legal challenges.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">The current ban restricts travellers from Iran, Libya, Somalia, Syria, Yemen, Venezuela and North Korea.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">And in January, the US has announced it was expanding its curbs on immigration to include six more countries. Citizens from Nigeria, Eritrea, Sudan, Tanzania, Kyrgyzstan and Myanmar will now be blocked from obtaining certain types of visas.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before: </b>Mr Trump said in September 2016 that he would reverse the deal President Barack Obama had struck to reopen diplomatic relations and improve trade.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>As president, he told an audience in Miami that he was "cancelling the Obama administration's one-sided deal." </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">In 2017, Mr Trump reimposed some trade and travel restrictions lifted by his predecessor. He kept the embassy open in Havana, although without naming an ambassador to the country.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Last year, the administration announced a ban on travel to Cuba for American group tours as well as cruise ships journeying to the island</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Until then, US tourism to Cuba was not permitted, but certain forms of organised group travel, known as "people-to-people" travel, had been allowed.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">This month the US administration announced further restrictions, saying it would suspend all private charter flights between the United States and Cuba, to increase economic pressure on Havana. The suspension comes into force on 13 October.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" data-component="image-block"><figure the Asian powerhouse of "raping" the US. China has been accused of suppressing the yuan to make its exports more competitive with US goods.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>In August 2019, the administration officially named China as a "currency manipulator". The US Treasury department defines currency manipulation as when countries deliberately influence the exchange rate between their currency and the US dollar to gain "unfair competitive advantage in international trade".</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">But in January, the US reversed its decision when China had agreed to refrain from devaluing its currency to make its own goods cheaper for foreign buyers.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><div class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before:</b> "I know the Wall Street people probably better than anybody knows them," <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" years".</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After:</b> Halfway through that eight-year promise, the US national debt has ballooned by more than a third, hitting $27tn in October 2020. Mr Trump increased the national debt ceiling in 2017, before suspending it until after the 2020 election in July 2019. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">It is predicted the debt will rise even further once the full economic impact of the coronavirus pandemic becomes apparent.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper ep2nwvo1" class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before: </b>Mr Trump repeatedly told his supporters that every single undocumented immigrant - of which there are estimated to be more than 11.3 million - "have to go".</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>As polling day approached, his stance began to soften slightly, then after the election he scaled it back to some two to three million deportations of people who "are criminal and have criminal records, gang members, drug dealers". </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">In fiscal year 2019 deportations were at 267,000, a slight rise on the year before, though not as high as the 2012 peak of 410,000 under the Obama administration. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Mr Trump's plans for immigration reform faced defeat this summer when the Supreme Court ruled against his administration's bid to rescind Deferred Action for Childhood Arrivals (Daca), which protects about 650,000 young people who entered the US without documents as children.</p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before: </b>The country's infrastructure "will become, by the way, second to none, and we will put millions of our people back to work as we rebuild it", he said in his victory speech in November.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>Has repeated his vow to spend big on the country's roads, rail and airports, but as yet, there is little sign of action. By March 2018 Congress had allocated $21bn for infrastructure spending - far short of the $1.5tn Mr Trump has called for. <a class="ssrcss-f6h2dj-InlineLink e1kn3p7n0" href="https://appropriations.house.gov/uploadedfiles/03.21.18_fy18_omnibus_-_infrastructure_-_one_pager.pdf?utm_source=Speaker.gov+Master+List&amp;utm_campaign=b11deee7b2-EMAIL_CAMPAIGN_2018_03_22&amp;utm_medium=email&amp;utm_term=0_3e173f5a25-b11deee7b2-157374621">The money will be spent on a wide range of upgrades and investments<span class="visually-hidden ssrcss-1f39n02-VisuallyHidden e16en2lz0">, <!-- -->external</span></a>, according to a congressional graphic.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">In April 2019, Mr Trump and Democratic leaders agreed to spend $2tn on infrastructure, an agreement that later fell apart. This June there were reports the Trump administration had a $1tn plan in the works, but no announcement has been made. </p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-10wcwg8-ComponentWrapper-FullWidthWrapper class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1o5p6v2-RichTextContainer e5tfeyi1"><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before:</b> Mr Trump repeatedly questioned the military alliance's purpose, calling it "obsolete". One issue that irked him was whether members were pulling their weight and "paying their bills". In one New York Times interview in July 2016, he even hinted that the US would not come to the aid of a member invaded by Russia.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After: </b>But as he hosted Nato's secretary general at the White House in April 2018, the US president said the threat of terrorism had underlined the alliance's importance. "I said it [Nato] was obsolete," Mr Trump said. "It's no longer obsolete."</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">In July 2018, Mr Trump reiterated his support at the Nato summit, but suggested the US might still leave if allies did not acquiesce to his budget demands. </p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">Mr Trump has continued to argue that Canada and European members of Nato  are not spending enough to support the alliance, and recently said the US will move nearly 12,000 troops out of Germany. </p></div></div><div class="ssrcss-suhx0k-RichTextComponentWrapper ep2nwvo0" data-component="text-block"><div class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">Before: </b>"Lock her up" was one of the main rallying cries of Mr Trump's supporters.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">They wanted to see Democratic rival Hillary Clinton in prison over the use of her private email server while secretary of state.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">And Mr Trump was more than willing to back their calls for, at the very least, a fresh investigation. During the debates, he told Mrs Clinton: "If I win, I am going to instruct my attorney general to get a special prosecutor to look into your situation."</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10"><b class="ssrcss-1xjjfut-BoldText e5tfeyi3">After:</b> The president-elect's tone changed almost as soon as he had won, describing the woman he had said was "such a nasty woman" as someone the country owed "a debt of gratitude". Later, he said he "hadn't given [the prosecution] a lot of thought" and had other priorities.</p><p class="ssrcss-1q0x1qg-Paragraph e1jhz7w10">In November 2016 Mr Trump's spokeswoman said he would not pursue a further investigation - to help Mrs Clinton "heal".</p></div></div></article></main><aside aria-hidden="true" aria-label="mpu-main" data-testid="mpu-main-aside-content"
